-*- Terms index -*-

  Prgs: progress of MCMC run (negative progress means burnin)
  Gage: gene-tree age proposal
  Gspr: gene-tree SPR proposal
  thet: species tree theta proposal
   tau: species tree tau proposal
   mix: mixing proposal
  mrte: migration rates proposal
mthet1: mean theta of node 0
mthet2: mean theta of node 1
mthet3: mean theta of node 2
 mtau1: mean tau of node 3
 mtau2: mean tau of node 4
 mmrt1: mean migration rate A -> B
 mmrt2: mean migration rate B -> A
log-PG: log-probability of gene trees (MSC)
 log-L: mean log-L of observing data

     |    Acceptance proportions     |
Prgs | Gage Gspr thet  tau  mix mrte | mthet1 mthet2 mthet3   mtau1  mtau2  mmrte1 mmrte2        log-PG           log-L
